Is it the same as an on-campus degree? </p>                <p class=\"horizontal-card-body\" style=\"color: #000000; font-style: normal; font-weight: 400; font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: -0.02em; line-height: 150%; text-transform: none; font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; -webkit-text-size-adjust: 100%; -ms-text-size-adjust: 100%; margin: 0 0 24px;\">                    Students who complete the programme will earn a master's degree. This degree will be the same as an on-campus degree. (No mention of online in the degree title). However, online mode of learning will be mentioned on the back side of the certificate, as per the guidelines of the University Grants Commission, Govt. of India. </p>                            </li>                                                                                                                                                                                                                               </ol>                  </td></tr>                                                                                                 <!-- END FAQ --> You’ll study contemporary <b>political, economic, and social</b> issues while building strong <b>analytical skills</b> and understanding how policies are made and managed.<br><br>In your first year, you’ll complete core courses for a broad foundation. In the second year, choose the <b>Data Analytics Track,</b> the <b>Policy Design Track,</b> or complete a <b>master’s dissertation</b> with faculty guidance.
